						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-cd3aa2b elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="cd3aa2b" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<h3 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Registered dietitians<br></h3>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-7e26e9d elementor-widget-laptop__width-initial elementor-widget-tablet__width-inherit elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="7e26e9d" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><span style="font-weight: 400">✔️ Have finished a minimum 5-year bachelor’s or master’s degree in dietetics and nutrition</span></p>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-ada1e43 elementor-widget-laptop__width-initial elementor-widget-tablet__width-inherit elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="ada1e43" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><span style="font-weight: 400">✔️ Undergo supervised practical training in various setting including hospital, universities, clinics, research labs, government agencies (a practicum of 9-12 months’ full time work)</span></p>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-468e134 elementor-widget-laptop__width-initial elementor-widget-tablet__width-inherit elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="468e134" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><span style="font-weight: 400">✔️ Are required by law to register with a provincial regulatory body—in BC, that’s the College of Health and Care Professionals of BC (CHCPBC)</span></p>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-ef108cc elementor-widget-laptop__width-initial elementor-widget-tablet__width-inherit elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="ef108cc" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><span style="font-weight: 400">✔️ Participate in continuing education and professional development mandated by the college</span></p>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-c53b06d elementor-widget-laptop__width-initial elementor-widget-tablet__width-inherit elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="c53b06d" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><span style="font-weight: 400">✔️ Blend ongoing professional training, clinical experience, and scientific evidence to create tailored food and nutrition plans</span></p>				</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>
				<div data-dce-background-color="#FFFFFF" class="elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-inner-column elementor-element elementor-element-80726d5" data-id="80726d5" data-element_type="column" data-e-type="column" data-settings="{&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;classic&quot;}">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-d876f93 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="d876f93" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<h3 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Nutritionists or influencers</h3>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-9a5eb38 elementor-widget-laptop__width-initial elementor-widget-tablet__width-inherit elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="9a5eb38" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><span style="font-weight: 400">❌ </span>In BC, anyone can call themselves a nutritionist, regardless of their education level.</p>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-0b71114 elementor-widget-laptop__width-initial elementor-widget-tablet__width-inherit elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="0b71114" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><span style="font-weight: 400">❌ May have only completed a short online course (even as little as 1 hour), while others may have no formal training at all. </span></p>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-772921a elementor-widget-laptop__width-initial elementor-widget-tablet__width-inherit elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="772921a" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><span style="font-weight: 400">❌ Do not have clinical experience in settings like hospitals or clinics, and may not have worked directly with patients managing medical conditions.</span></p>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-c7f7250 elementor-widget-laptop__width-initial elementor-widget-tablet__width-inherit elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="c7f7250" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><span style="font-weight: 400">❌ Are likely to have developed their expertise through their own personal experience, which may not be applicable to you</span></p>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-d19e431 elementor-widget-laptop__width-initial elementor-widget-tablet__width-inherit elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="d19e431" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><span style="font-weight: 400">❌ Are unregulated—most are independent business owners and are not obligated by law to keep up with professional development, or subject to health standards by a regulatory body </span></p>				</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>
					</div>
		</section>
					</div>
		</div>
					</div>
		</section>
				<section class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-ef8ac58 elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="ef8ac58" data-element_type="section" data-e-type="section" data-settings="{&quot;jet_parallax_layout_list&quot;:[],&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;classic&quot;}">
						<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
					<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-7a5376d" data-id="7a5376d" data-element_type="column" data-e-type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-13a79f2 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="13a79f2" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Featured BC Dietitians</h2>				</div>

				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<p class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">The top BC dietitians on our platform</p>				</div>
